<script type="text/javascript" src="//ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/1.8.3/jquery.min.js"></script>
<script src="//common.collegeboard.org/globalHeaderFooter/v2/js/cb.ghf.js" type="text/javascript"></script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var CB_JS_API = CB_JS_API || {};
 
CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH = (function () {
    
	//The current value of the autosuggest box
	var currentValue = "";

	//The callback passed to the name search api
	var cb = null;

	//The api key passed to the xml gateway.
	var apiKey = "";

	//The base url of the service call
	/****** IMPORTANT: this url needs to be changed as part of the release process, depending on what it should point to in prod ********/ 
	var baseUrl = "https://apiext.collegeboard.org/bscsuggestions/suggestions?q=";
	
	//The cached current result set, used to check for exact match
	var currentResults = null;

	/**
	 * @name fetchResults
	 * @description Implements the jsonp call to bscollege to get a json response containing the bscollege results.
	 * 
	 */
	function fetchResults () {
				
		var src = baseUrl+currentValue+"&api-key="+apiKey+"&callback=CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.parseResults";
		
		var jsonpTag = document.getElementById("jsonpTag");
		if(jsonpTag) {
		    document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].removeChild(jsonpTag);   
		}
		var scriptTag = document.createElement("script");
		scriptTag.setAttribute("id", "jsonpTag");
		scriptTag.src = src;
		document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].appendChild(scriptTag);
	}
	
	/**
	 * @name parseResults
	 * @description Parses the results of the fetchResults jsonp request and passes it to the callback supplied to
	 * the getCollegeInfo call
     * @param {Object} json The json string returned from BSCollege matching the given query.
     * 
	 */
	function _parseResults(json) {
	    if (cb && typeof(cb) == "function") {
    		if (!json) {
    		    cb(-1);
    		} else {
    		    currentResults = json.suggestionResponses;
                cb(currentResults);    
    		}    			        
	    }
	}
    
    /**
     * @name getSuggestions
     * @description This is the function called from the user of this API to get the college name search
     * information.  A json object is returned from the jsonp call and passed to the given callback function.
     * @param {Object} val the value to search on
     * @param {Object} cb the callback function to pass the search results.
     */
	function _getSuggestions(val, callback) {
		// invocation delay in millisecs
		var invocationDelay = 100;
		currentValue = val;
		cb = callback;
		setTimeout(fetchResults, invocationDelay);
	}
	
	/**
	 * @name goToProfile
	 * @description Redirects the page to the BigFuture college profile page of the given id.
     * @param {Object} id the id of the college to see.
	 */
	function _goToProfile(id, collegeName) {

	    newLocation = "https://bigfuture.collegeboard.org/college-profile?id="+id+"&searchType=site_qfs&tp=bf&bf_cat=college";
        if(collegeName)
        {
            newLocation += "&q="+collegeName;
        }
	    window.location = newLocation
	}
	
	/**
	 * @name goToSearch
	 * @description Redirects the page to the BigFuture site search page if there is not an exact match
	 * of one college in the result set.  If there is an exact match, redirects to that profile.
     * @param {String} val the value of the text box to use for site search 
	 */
	function _goToSearch(val) {
        if (!val) return;
        newLocation = "http://sitesearch.collegeboard.org/?q="+val+"&searchType=site_qfs&tp=bf&bf_cat=college";
	    window.location = newLocation;
	}
	
	/**
	 * @name setApiKey
	 * @description Sets the api key variable to be sent along with the service request.  This must be called before any functionality
	 * can be accessed
     * @param {String} key the api key.
	 */
	function _setApiKey(key) {
        apiKey = key;
    }
    
    return {
    	setApiKey: _setApiKey,
    	goToProfile: _goToProfile,
    	goToSearch: _goToSearch,
    	getSuggestions: _getSuggestions,
    	parseResults: _parseResults
    };
}())


/**
 * Global Object which all College Board properties and methods will extend from.
 *
 * FOO TEST
 * @namespace   CB
 * @author      UI Development Team
 */
if (typeof CB === 'undefined' || !CB) {
    var CB = {};
}

/**
 * TODO Remove, set-up locally
 */
jQuery.ajaxSetup({ cache:false });

/**
 * Checks for property in object
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param   {object} o Object to check
 * @param   {string} key Key value of object property
 * @return  {boolean} Result 
 */
CB.inObj = function (o, key) {
    return o.hasOwnProperty(key);
}; 

/**
 * Checks if object is boolean
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param {mixed} mixed Object to test
 * @return {boolean} Result 
 */
CB.isBoolean = function(mixed) {
    return typeof mixed === 'boolean';
};

/**
 * Checks for empty string
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param {string} str String to test 
 * @return {boolean} Result
 */
CB.isEmpty = function(str) {
    return !/\S/.test(str || '') || true;
};

/**
 * Checks for null value
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param {mixed} mixed Object to test
 * @return {boolean} Result
 */
CB.isNull = function(mixed) {
    return mixed === null;
};

/**
 * Checks for number
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param {mixed} mixed Object to test 
 * @return {boolean} Result
 */
CB.isNumber = function(mixed) {
    return typeof mixed === 'number' && isFinite(mixed);
};

/**
 * Checks for object
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param {mixed} mixed Object to test 
 * @return {boolean} Result
 */
CB.isObject = function(mixed) {
    return typeof mixed === 'object';
};

/**
 * Checks for string
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param {mixed} mixed Object to test
 * @return {boolean} Result
 */
CB.isString = function(mixed) {
    return typeof mixed === 'string';
};

/**
 * Check for undefined
 *
 * @public
 * @static
 * @param {mixed} mixed Object to test
 * @return {boolean} Result 
 */
CB.isUndefined = function(mixed) {
    return typeof mixed === 'undefined';
};

/**
 * Namespaced collection of utility methods
 *
 * @namespace   CB.utils 
 * @public
 * @static
 * @author      UI Development Team
 */
CB.utils = (function ($C) {	

    /**
     * @memberOf    CB.utils
     * @public
     * @static
     */
    return {

        /**
         * This method when called extracts any URL query string params into a key/value representation
         * object notation.
         *
         * @method getParams
         * @param {string} href String of representing anchor href value to be 
         * @return {object} Resulting objective  
         * @author Terrence Lee
         */
        getParams: function (href) {
            var i = 0, 
                paramsObj = {}, 
                paramsArray = [];

            if (!/\?/.test(href)) {
                return null;
            }

            paramsArray = href.split('?')[1].split('&');
            
            for (i; i < paramsArray.length; i++) {
                paramsObj[paramsArray[i].split('=')[0]] = paramsArray[i].split('=')[1];
            }

            return paramsObj;
        },

        /**
         * This method when called will verify if a particular key/value pair is found
         * in the query string.  If it exists override it with the passed in key/value pair.
         * If it is not found, simply add the respect key/value pair to the query string.
         *
         * In addition this method will store the query string parmaters return from the getPrams
         * util and store that returned object onto the current DOM element in the iteration
         * via the jQuery Data method.
         *
         * @method setParams
         * @see getParms
         * @param {array} elms Array of DOM elements
         * @param {object} params Object reference of query string params to check for
         * @param {boolean} [remove] Optional flag to represent removal of param
         * @example CB.utils.setParams(jQuery('.domElements'), {'decorator': 'none', 'pageId': 'abc'});
         * @author Terrence Lee
         */
        setParams: function (elms, params, remove) {
            var that = this, 
                key = null,
                currHref = null,
                currHrefParams = {},
                currHrefParamCount = 0;

            jQuery(elms).each(function () {

                currHref = jQuery(this).attr('href');

                currHrefParams = that.getParams(currHref);

                if (currHrefParams) { // Found params
                    
                    jQuery(this).data('queryParams', currHrefParams);

                    for (var key in params) {

                        if (!$C.inObj(params, key)) {
                            continue;
                        }

                        currHref = jQuery(this).attr('href');

                        if (typeof (currHrefParams[key]) !== 'undefined') {
                            var regEx = new RegExp(key + "\=" + currHrefParams[key]);
                            if (!remove) {
                                currHref = currHref.replace(regEx, key + "=" + params[key]);
                            } else if (remove) {
                                currHref = currHref.replace(regEx, '');
                                //Nothing left to remove, remove ?
                                if (jQuery(currHrefParams).length == 1) {
                                    currHref = currHref.replace('?', '');
                                }
                            }
                            jQuery(this).attr('href', currHref);
                        } else {
                            if (!remove) {
                                jQuery(this).attr('href', currHref + '&' + key + '=' + params[key]);
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    currHrefParams = {};

                } else { // No params, set whatever is passed in

                    for (var key in params) {
                        if (!$C.inObj(params, key)) {
                            continue;
                        }

                        currHref = jQuery(this).attr('href');
                        jQuery(this).attr('href', currHref + ((currHrefParamCount > 0) ? '&' : '?') + key + '=' + params[key]);
                        currHrefParamCount += 1;
                    }
                    currHrefParamCount = 0;
                }
            });
        },

        /**
         * Auto fires window print dialog when class match is found.
         *
         * @method  printPage
         * @param   {String} id      Id of element to match for auto print 
         * @param   {String} klass   Reserved class for auto firing print window dialog
         * @author  Nick Porochina, Terrence Lee
         * TODO Let's make this class name based only.
         */
        printPage: function(id, className) {
            if (jQuery('#' + id).hasClass(className)) {
                window.print();
                return false;
            }
        },

        /**
         * This is a simple utils method that either adds a new image to the dom, or will check the
         * passed parameter DOM element for a background image, and swap it to actual inline image.
         * Use primarily as a printer helper for printing background images.
         *
         * @method  addOrSwpImg
         * @param   {Object} o          Anonymous object of options
         * @option  {Object} el         DOM Element to act on
         * @option  {String} [klass]    Optional class to add to the generated image
         * @option  {String} [imgSrc]   Optional img src path for the image when a CSS background-image is not to be used
         * @author  Nick Porochina, Terrence Lee
         */
        addOrSwpImg: function(o) {
            var regEx;

            if(!o.imgSrc) {
                // Removing all characters in the css background-image value except for the img path
                regEx = /^.*?(\/img.*?)\"?\)$/g.test(o.el.css('background-image')); 
                o.imgSrc = RegExp.$1; 
            }

            jQuery('<img src="' + o.imgSrc + '" />').appendTo(o.el).addClass(o.klass || '');
        },


        /**
         * Standard wrapper method for handling browser pop-ups
         *
         * @method  browserPopUp
         * @param   {Object} elm          DOM Anchor Element, with valid HREF
         * @param   {Object} [o]          Anonymous object of options to set window properties
         * @option  {Number} [width]
         * @option  {Number} [height]
         * @option  {String} [resizable]
         * @option  {String} [scrollbars]
         * @option  {String} [menubar]
         * @option  {String} [toolbar]
         * @option  {String} [location]   Location chrome
         * @option  {String} [name]       Window name
         * @author  Nick Porochina, Terrence Lee
         */
        browserPopUp: function(elm, o) {
                var options = {
                    'width': 800,
                    'height': 750,
                    'resizable': 'yes',
                    'scrollbars': 'yes',
                    'menubar': 'no',
                    'toolbar': 'no',
                    'location': 'no',
                    'name': 'browserPopUp'
                },
                windowVars,
                newBrowserWindow;

                if (!elm[0]) {
                    return false;
                }

                jQuery.extend(options, (o = o || {}));
                o = options;

                //TODO Build from object  options
                jQuery(elm).click(function () {
                    windowVars = 'width=' + o.width + ',height=' + o.height + ',resizable=' + o.resizable + ',scrollbars=' + o.scrollbars + ',menubar=' + o.menubar + ',toolbar=' + o.toolbar + ',location=' + o.locationChrome;
                    newBrowserWindow = window.open(elm.attr('href'), o.name, windowVars);
                    newBrowserWindow.focus();
                    return false;
                });
        },



        /**
         * Simple wrapper to handle setting up SuckerFish JavaScript for MSIE, 
         * or browsers that do not suppor the :hover pseudo class.
         *
         * @method  sfHover
         * @param   {Array} sfEls  Array of jQuery selected DOM list elements to act upon
         * @author  Terrence Lee
         */
        sfHover: function (sfEls) {

            //TODO IE <7 ?
            if (!jQuery.browser.msie) {
                return false;
            }

            sfEls.each(function () {
                this.onmouseout = function () { jQuery(this).removeClass('sfhover'); };
                this.onmouseover = function () { jQuery(this).addClass('sfhover'); };
            });
        },


        /**
         * Single point of source for SWF Object
         *
         * @method  swfObject
         * @param   {object} options Object of options for swfObject
         * @author  Terrence Lee
         *
		 * Object Params: 
		 * swfUrl 	(String, required) specifies the URL of your SWF
		 * id 		(String, required) specifies the id of the HTML element 
						(containing your alternative content) you would like to have replaced by your Flash content
		 * width 	(String, required) specifies the width of your SWF
		 * height 	(String, required) specifies the height of your SWF
		 * version 	(String, required) specifies the Flash player version your SWF is 
						published for (format is: "major.minor.release" or "major")
		 * expressInstallSwfurl 	(String, optional) specifies the URL of your express install SWF and 
										activates Adobe express install. Please note that express install 
										will only fire once (the first time that it is invoked), that it is 
										only supported by Flash Player 6.0.65 or higher on Win or Mac platforms, 
										and that it requires a minimal SWF size of 310x137px.
		 * flashvars 	(Object, optional) specifies your flashvars with name:value pairs
		 * params 		(Object, optional) specifies your nested object element params with name:value pairs
		 * attributes 	(Object, optional) specifies your object's attributes with name:value pairs
		 * callbackFn 	(JavaScript function, optional) can be used to define a callback function that is 
						called on both success or failure of embedding a SWF file (see API documentation)
		 *
		 * Implmenetation:
         * swfobject.embedSWF(swfUrl, id, width, height, version, expressInstallSwfurl, flashvars, params, attributes, callbackFn)
         */
        swfObject: function (options) {
            var o, defaultOptions;

            defaultOptions = {
                'swfUrl': null, 
                'id': 'swfObjectDiv',
                'width': '300',
                'height': '300',
                'version': '9',
                'params': {
					'menu': 'false',
					'scale': 'noScale',
					'wmode': 'opaque',
					'allowFullScreen': 'true',
					'allowScriptAccess': 'always'
				},
                'expressInstallSwfurl': "//common.collegeboard.org/swf/expressInstall.swf", 
                'flashvars': null,
                'attributes': null,
                'callbackFn': null
            };

            o = jQuery.extend(defaultOptions, options);

            swfobject.embedSWF(o.swfUrl, o.id, o.width, o.height, o.version, o.expressInstallSwfurl, o.flashvars, o.params, o.attributes, o.callbackFn)
        }

    };

})(CB);
 
/**
 * This is a the 'twirl' wrapper method used for showing/hiding expandle content on the page.
 * It makes use of custom jQuery methods for toggling, that binds to a custom trigger class
 * of '.toTwirl'.  Requires no parameters, this is a wrapper method to handle bindings for 
 * the respective DOM elements.
 *
 * @static
 * @public
 * @function
 * @author      Armchair, Stephen Liu, Terrence Lee
 */
CB.twirl = function (options) {

    /**
     * Default global options
     */
    var config = {};
    config.scope = 'body'; //Scope of where twirls are bound, to body by default, allows limiting scope to different element
    config.noScroll = false; //Turns off all scrolling functionality when twirl is opened when passed in as true.  Set to false by default.

    jQuery.extend(config, options);

    /**
     * Changes the default easing from jQuery's "swing" to one of the Robert Penner equasions.
     *
     * @memberOf    jQuery
     * @type        String
     * @public
     * @static
     */
	jQuery.easing.def = 'easeOutQuad';

	jQuery('.toTwirl:not(.open)', config.scope).hide();

    /**
     * Toggle the hide and show content. jQuery method that bind to DOM elements not 'twirled', or opened. 
     *
     * @memberOf    jQuery
     * @type        Method
     * @public
     * @static
     *
     * @param       {Function} arguments[0]  Callback function handling showing of respective bound DOM element.
     *                  Also set's appropriate aria attributes.
     * @param       {Function} arguments[1]  Callback function handling hiding of respecitve bound DOM element.
     *                  Also set's appropriate aria attributes.
     */
    jQuery('.twirler:not(.twirled)', config.scope).toggle(
        function(){
            var stuffToTwirl;
            var twirlEl = this;
            jQuery(this).addClass('twirled');
            stuffToTwirl = jQuery(this).attr('href');			
            stuffToTwirl = cleanHREF(stuffToTwirl);
            jQuery(stuffToTwirl).attr('aria-hidden', 'false').slideDown('fast', function () {

                if(!jQuery(twirlEl).hasClass('.noScroll') && config.noScroll === false) {
                    jQuery(stuffToTwirl).scrollTo(500, function () { omnitureCallback(twirlEl); });
                }

                if (jQuery(twirlEl).hasClass('twirl') && !jQuery(twirlEl).attr('initOmni')) {
                    jQuery(twirlEl).attr('initOmni','1');
                } else if (jQuery(twirlEl).attr('initOmni')) {
                    jQuery(twirlEl).attr('initOmni','');
                }

            });
        },
        function(){
            var stuffToTwirl;

            jQuery(this).removeClass('twirled');
            stuffToTwirl = jQuery(this).attr('href');
            stuffToTwirl = cleanHREF(stuffToTwirl);
            jQuery(stuffToTwirl).attr('aria-hidden', 'true').slideUp('fast');
        }
    );

    var omnitureCallback = function (twirlEl) {
        if (typeof options !== 'undefined' && options.omniture && !jQuery(twirlEl).attr('initOmni')) {
            CB.omniture.init({
                'callee': twirlEl,
                'type': 'inlineView',
                'actionTitle': jQuery(twirlEl).html()
            });
        }
    };

    /**
     * Third Party binding for opening twirler objects from other objects on the page
     * via the twirlerThirdParty class name.  Place the aformentioned class name
     * on any anchor element that should fire a twriler element.  The href
     * of the third party link should be the same href value of the original
     * twirler object.
     *
     * @type    Method
     * @public
     * @static
     * @author  Terrence
     */
    jQuery('.twirlerThirdParty', config.scope).click(function () {

        var stuffToTwirl = jQuery(this).attr('href');
        stuffToTwirl = cleanHREF(stuffToTwirl);
        thirdPartyTwirl(stuffToTwirl);

        return false;
    });

    /**
     * Third Party helper function utilized by onload and thrid party element clicks that take you
     * to a twirl.
     *
     * @type    Function
     * @public
     * @private
     * @param {string} stuffToTwirl This is the id fragment string, '#id'
     * @author  Terrence
     */
    var thirdPartyTwirl = function (stuffToTwirl) {

        var twirlElm, twirlElmOpen;

        if (!stuffToTwirl) {
            return false;
        } 

        twirlElm = jQuery('.twirler:not(.twirled)[href=' + stuffToTwirl + ']', config.scope);

        //Parents?
        twirlElm.parents('.toTwirl').each(function () {
            jQuery('.twirler:not(.twirled)[href=#' + this.id + ']', config.scope).click();
        });
        
        twirlElm.click();

        //If we have open elements, don't activate again, but smooth scroll down
        twirlElmOpen = jQuery('.twirler:is(.twirled)[href=' + stuffToTwirl + ']', config.scope);
        if (twirlElmOpen[0]) {
            jQuery(stuffToTwirl).scrollTo(500);
        }

    };

    var cleanHREF = function (href) {

        if (/^htt.*$/i.test(href)) {
            href =  '#' + href.split('#')[1];
        } 

        return href;
    };

    //If should be open
	jQuery('.twirler.twirl', config.scope).click();

    //Init
    setTimeout(function () { thirdPartyTwirl(window.location.hash); }, 1000);
};

/**
 * This is the jqModal Singleton wrapper class for handling modals on collegeboard.org.  It
 * utilizes the jqModal jQuery minimalist modal plugin.  Explaination of that respective 
 * plugin is outside the scope of this documentation.  
 *
 * For further information on jqModal please see:
 * http://dev.iceburg.net/jquery/jqModal/
 *
 * A primary goal of the wrapper was to insure accessibility standards were met in our implementation.
 * These primarily entail setting up the modals either via Ajax, by hijacking the bound anchor
 * elements href attribute for the taret of the modal content, or via inline content.  As of
 * current, CB modals are handled entirely via the ajax method.  When JavaScript is disabled,
 * all links have still have a valid target page, that will behave in a traditional manner by opening
 * in a new window. Inline support will be added with a per need basis.
 *
 * The CB Modal wrapper class contains a predefined set of CSS class name based triggers to
 * handle automatic initalization of DOM elements that target modals, on page load. *
 * These triggers set-up with minimal effort a standard set of actions to happen when a an event 
 * bound Anchor DOM element is targetted.  Auto firing on DOM ready is also supported via 
 * exposed query string parameters on the parent page.
 *
 * At current there are four class name triggers, that when exposed in the DOM, will automatically
 * be assigned thier respective actions to handle modal actions.  All elements targeted with these
 * classes should valid anchors, with valid href attributes. It's important to note that all triggers
 * are recursive.  I.e., if found in loaded modal content, the same initializations will happen within 
 * context of the newly loaded DOM chunk.
 *
 * <strong>CSS Class Triggers</strong>
 *
 * <em>.cbmTriggerXHR</em>
 * This trigger should be added to anchor elements whose modal content will need additional XHR support.
 * For example, modals that require form posts, handling responses within the same modal.   
 *
 * <em>.cbmTriggerFlat</em>
 * Single state, yet complex modal.
 *
 * <em>.cbmTriggerStatic</em>
 * Primarily to be used for tooltip/static content. This trigger should be bound to elements loading documented
 * help text.  Anchors require valid fragments for locating help snippet from XHR response dom chunk.
 *
 * <em>.cbmTriggerReturn</em>
 * To be added to links that require an auto-fired modal on returning to the page.  This trigger will append
 * a predefined query string param, that can be passed back to the page upon returning from another page.
 * This assumes that upon returning the page a valid trigger from above has been applied to the anchor it 
 * is referencing.
 *
 * <strong>Query String Options</strong>
 * In addition each trigger type will look for predefined optional query string params on the HREF value.
 *
 * <em>'Hard Close'</em>: _hc=1
 * When found, closing the modal will force a hard refresh of the page.
 *
 * <em>'Class Override'</em>: _co='classRef'
 * All modals by default share a default set of CSS rules.  In the instance where
 * a modals style needs to be overridden, pass the class reference via this options.
 * Please note, in order to try to preven spoofing, the 'classRef' will be prepended
 * with 'cbm', ex., 'cbmclassRef'
 *
 * @public
 * @static
 * @author      Terrence Lee
 */

CB.jqmWrapper = (function ($C) {

    /**
     * This is the trigger map.  It houses all self contain callback methods to
     * hanlde actions at the respective states of modal action.  In addition,
     * each contains a property of 'type' to let class know during set-up
     * what type of initialization set-up should be accounted for.
     * The type property order matters.  Prep should always come last.
     *
     * @private
     * @static
     */
    var modalKlassTriggerMap = {
        'cbmTriggerXHR': { 
            type:   ['ajax', 'prep'], 
            onShow: ['cbModalShow'], 
            onLoad: ['cbModalChecks', 'cbModalXHR', 'cbModalTrack', 'cbModalAria'], 
            onHide: ['cbModalHide', 'cbModalAria'],
            prep:   ['cleanFragmentIdentifier'] 
        },
        'cbmTriggerInline': { 
            type:   ['inline'], 
            onShow: ['cbModalShow', 'cbModalChecks', 'cbModalTrack', 'cbModalAria'], 
            onHide: ['cbModalHide', 'cbModalAria']
        },
        'cbmTriggerFlat': { 
            type:   ['ajax', 'prep'], 
            onShow: ['cbModalShow'], 
            onLoad: ['cbModalChecks', 'cbModalTrack', 'cbModalAria'], 
            onHide: ['cbModalHide', 'cbModalAria'],
            prep:   ['cleanFragmentIdentifier'] 
        },
        'cbmTriggerStatic': {
            type:   ['ajax', 'prep'], 
            onShow: ['cbModalShow'], 
            onLoad: ['cbModalChecks', 'cbModalTrack', 'cbModalAria'], 
            onHide: ['cbModalHide', 'cbModalAria'],
            prep:   ['cleanFragmentIdentifier'] 
        },
        'cbmTriggerReturn': {
            type:   ['prep'], 
            prep:   ['addReturnParam']
        }
    },

    /**
     * An array of active page level modals.  Active meaning: visible.
     *
     * @type {array}
     * @private
     * @static
     */
    activeModals = [],

    /**
     * This is where extented methods can be added.  It is exposed via the 
     * customize method.
     *
     * @type {object}
     * @private
     * @static
     */
    customConf = {},

    /**
     * Class function variable initializations.
     */
    customize,
    init,
    helpers,
    actions,
    actionsManager;

    /**
     * This is the public facing init method.  This handles all 
     * initializations for triggered DOM elements.
     *
     * @type    {Function}
     * @param   {Object}    [domChunk]  Optional DOM context to search for class name triggers
     * @public
     * @static
     */
    init = function (domChunk) {

        var key,
            i,
            workers,
            domChunk,
            context;
        
        context = domChunk ? domChunk : jQuery('body');

        /**
         * Workers object.  Houses configuration worker methods for initalization.
         *
         * type {Object}
         */
        workers = {

            /**
             * This is the main modal configuration method for setting up DOM mark-up for 
             * ajax modals, and attaching to the jqmModal plugin.
             *
             * @type    {Method}
             * @param   {String}   klass   Represents object 'key' for seting up the modal.  
             *                             Key is a string reference to the predefined trigger 
             *                             class names.  See call for context.
             */
            ajaxModalConfig: function (klass) {
                var modalId = klass + 'Modal', url;

                // Check if modal exists by this Id, and global class reference of .cbModal
                if (!jQuery('div#' + modalId + '.cbModal')[0]) {
                    jQuery('<div role="dialog" aria-hidden="true" id="' + modalId + '" class="jqmWindow cbModal roundies"><a class="cbmCloseX cbmClose" role="button" tabindex="0">Close</a><div class="cbmContents"><div class="cbmLoader"></div></div></div>').appendTo('body');
                // Else begin abstract increment, and create new modal Id, based on current context type length
                } else {
                    modalId = modalId + jQuery('div#' + modalId + '.cbModal').length;
                    jQuery('<div role="dialog" aria-hidden="true" id="' + modalId + '" class="jqmWindow cbModal roundies"><a class="cbmCloseX cbmClose" role="button" tabindex="0">Close</a><div class="cbmContents"><div class="cbmLoader"></div></div></div>').appendTo('body');
                }

                // @see CB.utils#setParams
                $C.utils.setParams(jQuery('.' + klass), {'decorator': 'none'});
                
                jQuery('.' + klass).hasClass('.cbmTriggerHandShake');
                
                // @see jQuery#jqm
                jQuery('div#' + modalId).jqm({
                    overlay: 40, 
                    ajax: '@href', 
                    //ajaxText: 'loading',
                    closeClass: 'cbmClose',
                    placeResponse: '.cbmContents',
                    loadingImage: '/img/ajax-loader.gif',
                    trigger: context.find('.' + klass), 
                    onShow: function (o) {actionManager('onShow', {'jqmObject': o});}, 
                    onLoad: function (o) {actionManager('onLoad', {'jqmObject': o});}, 
                    onHide: function (o) {actionManager('onHide', {'jqmObject': o});}
                })
            },

            /**
             * This is the main modal configuration method for setting handling any type of
             * prep work that needs to happen to a respective targetted Anchor element.
             * to the jqmModal plugin.
             *
             * @type    {Method}
             * @param   {String}   klass   Represents object property 'key' for seting up the modal.  
             *                             Key is a string reference to the predefined trigger 
             *                             class names.  See call for context.
             */
            relatedTriggersConfig: function (klass) {
                actionManager('prep', {'cbmTriggerKlass': klass});
            },

            //TODO: Comment
            inlineModalConfig: function (klass) { 

                var modalId = klass + 'Modal';

                // Check if modal exists by this Id, and global class reference of .cbModal
                if (!jQuery('div#' + modalId + '.cbModal')[0]) {
                    jQuery('<div role="dialog" aria-hidden="true" id="' + modalId + '" class="jqmWindow cbModal roundies"><a class="cbmCloseX cbmClose" role="button" tabindex="0">Close</a><div class="cbmContents"><div class="cbmLoader"></div></div></div>').appendTo('body');
                // Else begin abstract increment, and create new modal Id, based on current context type length
                } else {
                    modalId = modalId + jQuery('div#' + modalId + '.cbModal').length;
                    jQuery('<div role="dialog" aria-hidden="true" id="' + modalId + '" class="jqmWindow cbModal roundies"><a class="cbmCloseX cbmClose" role="button" tabindex="0">Close</a><div class="cbmContents"><div class="cbmLoader"></div></div></div>').appendTo('body');
                }

                // @see CB.utils#setParams
                $C.utils.setParams(jQuery('.' + klass));
                // Clearn params
                jQuery('.' + klass).each(function () {
                    $(this).attr('href', $(this).attr('href').split('?')[0]);
                });

                // @see jQuery#jqm
                jQuery('div#' + modalId).jqm({
                    overlay: 40, 
                    closeClass: 'cbmClose',
                    placeResponse: '.cbmContents',
                    trigger: context.find('.' + klass), 
                    onShow: function (o) {actionManager('onShow', {'jqmObject': o});}, 
                    onHide: function (o) {actionManager('onHide', {'jqmObject': o});}
                })

            },

            //TODO: Modal from modal
            recursiveModalConfig: function (klass) { }

        };

        /**
         * This is the brain of the class.  By looping through the modalTrigger map keys, 
         * which are the trigger class names, and checking each key against the DOM
         * respective class name triggers.
         */
        for (klass in modalKlassTriggerMap) {
            if ($C.inObj(modalKlassTriggerMap, klass) && context.find('.' + klass)[0]) { 
                for (i = 0; i < modalKlassTriggerMap[klass].type.length; i++) {
                    if (typeof (modalKlassTriggerMap[klass].type) !== 'undefined' && modalKlassTriggerMap[klass].type[i] === 'ajax') {
                        workers.ajaxModalConfig(klass);
                    } else if (typeof (modalKlassTriggerMap[klass].type) !== 'undefined' && modalKlassTriggerMap[klass].type[i] === 'inline') {
                        workers.inlineModalConfig(klass);
                    } else if (typeof (modalKlassTriggerMap[klass].type) !== 'undefined' && modalKlassTriggerMap[klass].type[i] === 'prep') {
                        workers.relatedTriggersConfig(klass);
                    }
                }

                helpers.autoFireHelper(klass);//Catch auto loaded modals
            }
        }

    };

    /**
     * This is the action manager for handling all modal functions.  It is given to the 
     * jqm plugin as a callback method for each for the predefined jqm plugin callback
     * states: 'onshow', 'onload', 'onhide'
     *
     * It is also invoked directly in the init method when prep work needs to occur
     * on a repspective triggering DOM element.
     *
     * The private variable 'actionsRef' will point to either the actions.callbacks, or
     * actions.prep depending on which object property is found on the object argument
     * passed to the actionManager call.
     *
     * Upon extracting class name from argument object, or calling DOM element, it will 
     * then use that class name to loop through the modalKlassTriggerMap firing the associated
     * actions for the deteremined callback state/or prep work.
     *
     * @name   actionManager
     * @type   {Function}
     * @see    CB.jqmWrapper#init
     *
     * @param  {String}  type               Type of callback that is invoking the actionManager: 
     *                                      'onShow', 'onHide', 'onLoad'
     *
     * @param  {Object}  o                  Action manager configuration argument object
     * @option {String}  [cbmTriggerKlass]  CSS Trigger Class name for an element. Used for prep work, invoked
     *                                      directly from init method.
     * @option {Object}  [jqmObject]        jqm Modal reference object passed from the respect callback action
     *      @option {Object}  w                  The DOM reference of the active modal window
     *      @option {Object}  t                  The DOM reference of the calling trigger element
     *
     * @private
     * @static
     */
    actionManager =  function (type, o) {
        var cbmTriggerKlass,
            actionsRef,
            i;
        
        if (typeof o.jqmObject !== 'undefined') {
            /\b(cbm\w+)\b/.test(o.jqmObject.t.className);
            cbmTriggerKlass = RegExp.$1;
            actionsRef = actions.callbacks;
        } else {
            cbmTriggerKlass = o.cbmTriggerKlass;
            actionsRef = actions.prep;
        }

        if (typeof modalKlassTriggerMap[cbmTriggerKlass] !== 'undefined') {
            for (i = 0; i < modalKlassTriggerMap[cbmTriggerKlass][type].length; i++) { 
                actionsRef[modalKlassTriggerMap[cbmTriggerKlass][type][i]](o.jqmObject || cbmTriggerKlass, modalKlassTriggerMap[cbmTriggerKlass][type], type);
            }

            //Check for exended options
            try {
                //First check for class options
                for (var key in customConf) {
                    if (!$C.inObj(customConf, key)) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (jQuery(o.jqmObject.t).hasClass('.' + key)) {
                        customConf[key].actions[type](o.jqmObject || cbmTriggerKlass, modalKlassTriggerMap[cbmTriggerKlass][type], type);
                    }
                }
                //Now try specific id'd options
                customConf[o.jqmObject.t.id].actions[type](o.jqmObject || cbmTriggerKlass, modalKlassTriggerMap[cbmTriggerKlass][type], type);
            } catch (e) {
                // Error
            }
        }
    };

    /**
     * Private object holding privately scoped modal actions: callbacks and prep.
     *
     * @name   actions
     * @type   {Object}
     * @see    actionsManager
     * @private
     * @static
     */
    actions = {

        /**
         * Object holding callback actions.
         *
         * @name   actions
         * @type   {Object}
         * @see    CB.jqmWrapper actionsManager, modalKlassTriggerMap
         */
        callbacks: {

            //TODO Comment
            cbModalChecks: function(o, callbacks, type) {
                var modalHeight;

                //TODO make placeResponse 'custom', and branch in jqModal
                if (!o.initComplete) {
                    if (o.c.ajax) {
                        $('<div class="_responseReplace" style="position:absolute; left: -9999px; width:' + o.w.width() + 'px">' + o.c.responseText + '</div>').appendTo(o.w.find(o.c.placeResponse));
                    } else {
                        $('<div class="_responseReplace" style="position:absolute; left: -9999px; width:' + o.w.width() + 'px;">' + jQuery(jQuery(o.t).attr('href')).html() + '</div>').appendTo(o.w.find(o.c.placeResponse));
                    }

                    modalHeight = o.w.find('._responseReplace').height() + 'px';
                    $(o.c.placeResponse, o.w).html(o.w.find('._responseReplace').html());
                }


                if (typeof (jQuery(o.t).data('queryParams')) !== 'undefined') {
                    //Parse response or link for various flags
                    if (typeof (jQuery(o.t).data('queryParams')['_hc']) !== 'undefined') { //Hard close refreshes window
                        if (jQuery('input#' +  jQuery(o.t).data('queryParams')['_hc'])[0]) {
                            o.cbmHardClose = true;
                        }
                    }

                    if (typeof (jQuery(o.t).data('queryParams')['_co']) !== 'undefined') { //CSS window overrides
                        jQuery(o.w).addClass('cbm' + jQuery(o.t).data('queryParams')['_co']);  
                    }

                    if (typeof (jQuery(o.t).data('queryParams')['_cm']) !== 'undefined') { //Mulitple contextual modals
                        modalHeight = jQuery('div#' + o.t.id + 'Content', o.w).height();
                        jQuery('div.cbmContextualModal[id!=' + o.t.id + 'Content]', o.w).hide();
                    }
                }

                if (!o.initComplete) {
                    $(o.c.placeResponse, o.w).css('visibility','hidden').animate(
                        {height: modalHeight}, 
                        function () { 
                            if (!$.browser.msie) {
                                $(this).hide().css('visibility','').fadeIn('fast');
                            } else {
                                $(this).css({'visibility': '', 'zoom': '1'});
                            }
                            $(this).css('height','');
                        }
                    );
                }

                /**
                 * Recursively look for new modals
                 * @see CB.jqmWrapper#init
                 */
                $C.jqmWrapper.init(jQuery(o.w));

                //Set the init complete flat
                o.initComplete = 1;
            },

            cbModalShow: function (o, callbacks, type) {
                //Set default initial height
                jQuery(o.w.find(o.c.placeResponse)).css('height', '150px');
                activeModals.push(o.w); 
                jQuery(o.w).show();
            },

            cbModalHide: function (o, callbacks, type) {
                //Allows for multiples
                if (activeModals.length > 1) {
                    o.w.fadeOut(
                        '500', 
                        function () { 
                            if (o.cbmHardClose) {
                                location.reload(); 
                            }
                            o.w.removeAttr('style');
                            jQuery(o.c.placeResponse).empty();
                        }
                    );
                } else {
                    o.w.fadeOut(
                        '500',
                        function(){ 
                            if (o.cbmHardClose) {
                                location.reload();
                            }
                            o.w.removeAttr('style');
                            jQuery(o.c.placeResponse).empty();
                        }
                    );
                }
                //Reset to false on hide
                o.initComplete = 0; 
                o.o.remove(); 
                activeModals.pop();
            },

            cbModalXHR: function(o, callbacks, type) {
                var that = this,
                    i = 0,
                    l = callbacks.length;

                $C.utils.setParams(jQuery('.cbmXHRState'), {'decorator': 'none'});

                o.w.jqmAddClose($(o.w.find('.' + o.c.closeClass), o.w));
                o.e(o.w);

                o.w.find('form').submit(function () {
                    var self = this;

                    jQuery.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',    
                        url: jQuery(self).attr('action'), 
                        data: jQuery(self).serialize(),
                        cache: false,
                        timeout: 5000,

                        beforeSend: function () {
                            jQuery(self).find('input, select, button, textarea').attr('disabled', 'true');
                        },

                        error: function (xhrObj, errorType) {
                            if (o.c.placeResponse) {
                                jQuery(o.w).find(o.c.placeResponse).html('There was an error processing this request.  Please close the window and try again later.');
                            } else {
                                jQuery(o.w).html('There was an error processing this request.  Please close the window and try again later.');
                            }
                        },

                        success: function (response) {   
                            if (o.c.placeResponse) {
                                jQuery(o.w).find(o.c.placeResponse).html(response);
                            } else {
                                jQuery(o.w).html(response);
                            }
                            actionManager('onLoad', {'jqmObject': o});
                            /*
                            for (i; i < l; i++) { 
                                that[callbacks[i]](o, callbacks);
                            }
                            */
                        }

                    });    

                    return false;
                });

                o.w.find('.cbmXHRState').bind('click', function () {
                    var self = this;

                    jQuery.ajax({
                        type: 'GET',
                        url: jQuery(self).attr('href'), 
                        cache: false,
                        timeout: 5000,

                        beforeSend: function () {
                            jQuery(self).unbind('click').bind('click', function () { return false;});
                        },

                        error: function (xhrObj, errorType) {
                            if (o.c.placeResponse) {
                                jQuery(o.w).find(o.c.placeResponse).html('There was an error processing this request.  Please close the window and try again later');
                            } else {
                                jQuery(o.w).html('There was an error processing this request.  Please close the window and try again later');
                            }
                        },

                        success: function (response) {   
                            if (o.c.placeResponse) {
                                jQuery(o.w).find(o.c.placeResponse).html(response);
                            } else {
                                jQuery(o.w).html(response);
                            }

                            for (i; i < l; i++) { 
                                that[callbacks[i]](o, callbacks);
                            }
                        }

                    });    
                    return false;
                });
                
            },

            cbModalAria: function (o, callbacks, type) {
                (type === 'onLoad') ? o.w.attr('aria-hidden', 'false') : o.w.attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
                helpers.focusCaptureHelper(type);
            },

            //TODO: Add tracking
            cbModalTrack: function (o, callbacks, type) { 
                /*
                var s = s_gi('clgbcollegeboardcomprod'),
                    bakPageName = false,
                    href = jQuery(o.t).attr('href');

                if (s.pageName) {
                    bakPageName = s.pageName;
                }
                
                if (/\?/.test(href)) {
                    href = href.split('?')[0];
                }

                s.pageName = 'modalPage: ' + href;
                s.t();

                if (bakPageName) {
                    s.pageName = bakPageName;
                }
                */
            }
        },

        /**
         * Object holding prep actions.
         *
         * @name   prep
         * @type   {Object}
         * @see    CB.jqmWrapper actionsManager, modalKlassTriggerMap
         */
        prep: {

            /**
             * Cleans anchor fragments in HREF value for IE jQuery XHR bug, i.e., '#anchor'
             *
             * @name   prep
             * @type   {Object}
             * @see    CB.jqmWrapper actionsManager, modalKlassTriggerMap
             */
            cleanFragmentIdentifier: function (key, callbacks, type) {
                var href, 
                    baseHref, 
                    query;

                //TODO: Convert to regex
                if (/\#/i.test(jQuery('.' + key).attr('href'))) {
                    jQuery('.' + key).each(function () {
                        href = jQuery(this).attr('href').split('#');
                        query = href[1].split('?')[1];
                        jQuery(this).attr('href', href[0] + '?' + query);
                    });
                }

            },

            addReturnParam: function (key, callbacks, type) {
                jQuery('.' + key).each(function () {
                    $C.utils.setParams(this, {'cbmRefId': this.id});
                });
            }

        }

    };

    /**
     * Helper methods used by callbacks.
     *
     * @name   helpers
     * @type   {Object}
     * @private
     * @static
     */
    helpers = {

        //TODO: Finish focus capture
        focusCaptureHelper: function (type) {
            if (type === 'onLoad') {
                jQuery(document).keydown( function( e ) {
                    if(e.which == 27) {  // escape, close box
                        jQuery(activeModals[activeModals.length-1]).jqmHide();
                    }
                }); 
            } else if (type === 'onHide'){
                jQuery(document).unbind('keydown');            
            }
        },

        autoFireHelper: function (klass) {
            //Via Query String
            if (/\bcbmRefId=(.*?\w+)\b&?/.test(window.location.search)) {
                jQuery('#' + RegExp.$1).click();
            }
            //Via target href query param
            jQuery('.' + klass).each(function () {
                if (typeof (jQuery(this).data('queryParams')) !== 'undefined') {
                    if (typeof (jQuery(this).data('queryParams')['_al']) !== 'undefined') { //Hard close refreshes window
                        jQuery(this).hide().click();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

    };

    /**
     * Method for allowing this object to be extending after initialization.
     * It's a way to add custom methods to be fired for specific DOM elements
     * that have already been targeted via a predefined trigger
     *
     * @type {Function}
     * @public
     * @static
     */
    customize = function (options) {
        jQuery.extend(customConf, options);
    };

    /**
     * Make public only what we have to!
     */
    return {
        init:    init,
        customize: customize
    };        

})(CB);


/**
 * XXX TODO COMMENT
 */
CB.omniture = (function ($C) {

    var init,
        pageView,
        inlineView,
        validateObj,
        trackIt;

    init = function (options) {
        if (typeof s !== 'undefined') {
            if (options.type === 'pageView') {
                pageView(options.properties);
            } else if (options.type === 'inlineView') {
                inlineView(options);
            }
        }
    };

    pageView = function (props) {
        var storedPageName = null;

        if (s.pageName) {
            storedPageName = s.pageName;
        }

        for (var key in props) {
            if (!$C.inObj(props, key)) {
                continue;
            }
            s[key] = props[key];
        }

        s.t();

        if (storedPageName) {
            s.pageName = storedPageName;
        }
    };

    inlineView = function (options) {
        //Only set-up for anchors now
        if (typeof s !== 'undefined') {
            s.linkTrackVars = 'prop44,eVar41'; 
            s.prop44 = s.pageName + ":" + options.actionTitle; 
            s.eVar41 = s.pageName + ":" + options.actionTitle;
            s.tl(options.callee, 'o', s.pageName + ":" + options.actionTitle);
        }
    };

    /**
     * Make public only what we have to!
     */
    return {
        init:    init
    };        


})(CB);
/**
 * Namespaced collection of utility methods
 *
 * @namespace   CB.utils 
 * @public
 * @static
 * @author      UI Development Team
 */
CB.utils = (function ($C) {	
    /**
     * @memberOf    CB.utils
     * @public
     * @static
     */
    return {
		/**
		 * Simple wrapper to handle setting up SuckerFish JavaScript for MSIE, 
		 * or browsers that do not suppor the :hover pseudo class.
		 *
		 * @method  sfHover
		 * @param   {Array} sfEls  Array of jQuery selected DOM list elements to act upon
		 * @author  Terrence Lee
		 */
		sfHover: function (sfEls) {

			//TODO IE <7 ?
			if (!jQuery.browser.msie) {
				return false;
			}

			sfEls.each(function () {
				this.onmouseout = function () { jQuery(this).removeClass('sfhover'); };
				this.onmouseover = function () { jQuery(this).addClass('sfhover'); };
			});
		}
	};
})(CB);

	$(".rightRailContent > .normalRailBox:even").addClass("rightRailWhiteBox");

	var content = $('#content').height()

	}
});  	

$(document).ready(function(){

    $('.searchBtn').click(function(){
        var parentcheck = $(this).parent().attr('id');

        if (parentcheck == "siteSearch"){

            if (($('#dynamicSearch').val() == "Search by Keyword") || ($('#dynamicSearch').val() == "") ){
                return false;
            } else {
                siteSearch.submit();
            }
            return false;
        }

    });


    $("#dynamicSearch").bind("keypress", function(e) {

         if(jQuery.browser.msie){
         
            if (($('#dynamicSearch').val() == "") && (e.keyCode == 13)){ 
                return false;
            }
         } else {
            if (e.which == "Search by Keyword") return false;
            if (e.which == "") return false;  
         }

    });

    // Check if the college search box is present in the page before init.
    if( $('#nameSearchBox').length ) {
        initNameSearchModule();
    }

});




//COLLEGE QUICKFINDER CODE



//Global variable for caching current results.  This couldn't be made a member variable of
//NameSearchModule because the callback from the jsonp request sets "this" to window, and is
//therefore out of scope.
var currentNameSearchResults;

/*
 * @name NameSearchModule
 * @constructor
 * This is the constructor for the name search module.
 */
function NameSearchModule() {
    var self_ = this;
    //Set api key for this module
	
	//PROD Api key
	CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.setApiKey("cbwww-e99be64d-d782-4fa7-a915-6a4a5b4185b2");
	
	
    
    this.searchBox = document.getElementById("nameSearchBox");
    
    //set min-width of autosuggest results based on input field width
    var width = this.searchBox.clientWidth;
    var style = "min-width: "+width+"px;";
    document.getElementById("nameSearchResponseList").setAttribute("style",style);
    
    function keyListener (evt) {
        self_.handleKeyUp(evt.keyCode);
    }
    
    //Add key up listeners for the search box.
    if (this.searchBox.addEventListener) {
        this.searchBox.addEventListener("keyup", keyListener, false);
    } else {
        this.searchBox.attachEvent("onkeyup", keyListener, false);
    }
    
    window.onunload = function () {
        var box = document.getElementById("nameSearchBox");
        if (box.removeEventListener) {
            box.removeEventListener("keyup", keyListener, false);
        } else if(box.detatchEvent) {
            box.detatchEvent("keyup", keyListener);            
        }
        box.value = "";
        currentNameSearchResults = null;
        resultsList = document.getElementById("nameSearchResponseList");
        while (resultsList.firstChild) {
            resultsList.removeChild(resultsList.firstChild);
        } 
    }
    
    //Add click listener for go button
    var goBtn = document.getElementById("nameSearchGoButton");
    if (goBtn.addEventListener) {
        goBtn.addEventListener("mouseup", function (evt) {
            if (evt.button != 0) return;
            CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.goToSearch(self_.searchBox.value);     
        }, false);        
    } else { //IE
        goBtn.attachEvent("onmouseup", function (evt) {
            if (evt.button != 1) return;
            CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.goToSearch(self_.searchBox.value);        
        });
    } 
}

/**
 * @name handleKeyUP
 * @description Handles the keystrokes on the input box.
 * @param {Number} keyCode the keyCode of the keypress event
 * 
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.handleKeyUp = function (keyCode) {
    if (keyCode === 38) { //up arrow
       this.focusListItemUp();       
    } else if (keyCode === 40) { //down arrow
       this.focusListItemDown();       
    } else if (keyCode === 13) { //enter key
       this.submitListSelection();       
    } else {
       this.populateResults(this.searchBox.value);            
    }
}

/**
 * @name submitListSelection
 * @description Handler for pressing the enter key in the search box.
 * If there is a focused list item, goes to that college profile, else goes
 * to site search with the value of the text box.
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.submitListSelection = function () {
    var current = this.findCurrentFocused();
    var self_ = this;
    if (current != -1) {
        if (currentNameSearchResults.length) {
            CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.goToProfile(currentNameSearchResults[current].id,
                    currentNameSearchResults[current].name);
        } else {
            CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.goToProfile(currentNameSearchResults.id,
                    currentNameSearchResults[current].name);
        }
    } else {
        CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.goToSearch(document.getElementById("nameSearchBox").value);
    }
}

/**
 * @name focusListItemUp
 * @description changes focus of the current list item to the previous item upon up arrow
 * press. 
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.focusListItemUp = function () {
    var res = this.getCurrentResults();
    if (res.length == 0) return;
    var current = this.findCurrentFocused(res);
    if (current === -1) {
        //Space in the name below is for use with any existing classes, so any existing ones
        //will be separated by a space.
        var currentClass = res[res.length - 1].getAttribute("class") || "";
        currentClass = currentClass + " focused";
        res[res.length - 1].setAttribute("class", currentClass);
		if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE 7.0") != -1) {
			res[res.length - 1].style.setAttribute("cssText", "background-color: #cccccc;");
		}
    } else {
        var currentClass = res[current].getAttribute("class") || "";
        currentClass = currentClass.replace("focused", "");
        res[current].setAttribute("class", currentClass);
		if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE 7.0") != -1) {
			res[current].style.setAttribute("cssText", "background-color: #ffffff;");
		}
        if (current == 0) {
            return;
        }
        var nextClass = res[current - 1].getAttribute("class") || "";
        nextClass = nextClass + " focused"
        res[current - 1].setAttribute("class", nextClass);
		if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE 7.0") != -1) {
			res[current - 1].style.setAttribute("cssText", "background-color: #cccccc;");
		}
    }
}

/**
 * @name focusListItemDown
 * @description changes focus of the current list item to the previous item upon down arrow
 * press. 
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.focusListItemDown = function () {
    var res = this.getCurrentResults();
    if (res.length == 0) return;
    var current = this.findCurrentFocused(res);
    if (current === -1) {
        var currentClass = res[0].getAttribute("class") || "";
        currentClass = currentClass + " focused";
        res[0].setAttribute("class", currentClass);
		if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE 7.0") != -1) {
			res[0].style.setAttribute("cssText", "background-color: #cccccc;");
		}
    } else {
        var currentClass = res[current].getAttribute("class") || "";
        currentClass = currentClass.replace("focused", "");
        res[current].setAttribute("class", currentClass);
		if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE 7.0") != -1) {
			res[current].style.setAttribute("cssText", "background-color: #ffffff;");
		}
        if (current == res.length - 1) {
            return;
        }
        var nextClass = res[current+1].getAttribute("class") || "";
        nextClass = nextClass + " focused"
        res[current + 1].setAttribute("class", nextClass);
		if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE 7.0") != -1) {
			res[current + 1].style.setAttribute("cssText", "background-color: #cccccc;");
		}
    }
}

/**
 * @name findCurrentFocused
 * @description Finds the currently focused list item and returns its index,
 * -1 otherwise 
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.findCurrentFocused = function (res) {
    if (!res) res = this.getCurrentResults();
    var idx = -1;
    var counter = 0;
    for (var i in res) {
        if (res[i].getAttribute("class") && res[i].getAttribute("class").indexOf("focused") >= 0) {
            idx = counter; 
        } else {
            counter++;
        }  
    }
    return idx;
}


/**
 * @name getCurrentResults
 * @description returns an array of the li nodes for the current search, if
 * there are any results
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.getCurrentResults = function () {
    var list = document.getElementById("nameSearchResponseList");
    var resultItems = [];
    var first = list.firstChild;
    if (first) {
        resultItems.push(first);
        var cur = first;
        while (cur.nextSibling) {
            resultItems.push(cur.nextSibling);
            cur = cur.nextSibling;
        }
    }
    return resultItems;
}

/**
 * @name populateResults
 * @description Called upon a character entered in the search box.  Calls the api's
 * entry point, which is getSuggestions, passing the current text box value and the 
 * callback to handle the results.
 * @param {String} val the current value of the search box.
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.populateResults = function (val) {
    if (val === "") {
        resultsList = document.getElementById("nameSearchResponseList");
		resultsList.className = resultsList.className.replace( /(?:^|\s)active(?!\S)/ , '' );
        while (resultsList.firstChild) {
            resultsList.removeChild(resultsList.firstChild);
        }
        return;
    }
    if (val.length >= 3) {
        CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.getSuggestions(val, this.populateAutoComplete);        
    }
}


/**
 * @name gotoProfile
 * @description calls the api method goToProfile with the id of the selected college
 * from the suggestion list.
 * This is a public function because the caller is a callback coming from the jsonp
 * request and is out of scope for this class
 * @param {Number} id the id of the selected college.
 * @Name of selected college {String} id the id of the selected college.
 */
function gotoProfile(id, collegeName, browser) {
    return function(evt) {
		if (browser === "ie") {//IE
			if (evt.button != 1) return;
		} else {
			if (evt.button != 0) return;
		}
		CB_JS_API.COLLEGE_SEARCH.goToProfile(id, collegeName);
    }
} 

/**
 * @name populateAutoComplete
 * @description parses the json response from the jsonp request and creates
 * the list from the results.  
 * @param {Object} json the json object returned from the name search api.
 */
NameSearchModule.prototype.populateAutoComplete = function (json) {
    if (json === -1 ) return;
    var resultsList = document.getElementById("nameSearchResponseList");
	resultsList.className = " active ";
    currentNameSearchResults = json;
    
    //clear list for new set
    while (resultsList.firstChild) {
        resultsList.removeChild(resultsList.firstChild);
    }
    
    //create list item and append to parent
    function createListItem(item) {
        var li = document.createElement("li");
        li.innerHTML = item.name;
        var id = item.id;
        var name = item.name;
        resultsList.appendChild(li);
        if (li.addEventListener) {
            li.addEventListener("mouseup", gotoProfile(id, name, "nonIe"), false);
        } else {//IE
            li.attachEvent("onmouseup", gotoProfile(id, name, "ie"));
        }
    }
    
    if (!json.length) { //handles single result case
        createListItem(json);
    } else {
        for (var i in json) {
            createListItem(json[i]);    
        }
    }
}




function initNameSearchModule() {
	new NameSearchModule();
}

YAHOO.util.Easing={easeNone:function(B,A,D,C){return D*B/C+A;},easeIn:function(B,A,D,C){return D*(B/=C)*B+A;},easeOut:function(B,A,D,C){return -D*(B/=C)*(B-2)+A;},easeBoth:function(B,A,D,C){if((B/=C/2)<1){return D/2*B*B+A;}return -D/2*((--B)*(B-2)-1)+A;},easeInStrong:function(B,A,D,C){return D*(B/=C)*B*B*B+A;},easeOutStrong:function(B,A,D,C){return -D*((B=B/C-1)*B*B*B-1)+A;},easeBothStrong:function(B,A,D,C){if((B/=C/2)<1){return D/2*B*B*B*B+A;}return -D/2*((B-=2)*B*B*B-2)+A;},elasticIn:function(C,A,G,F,B,E){if(C==0){return A;}if((C/=F)==1){return A+G;}if(!E){E=F*0.3;}if(!B||B<Math.abs(G)){B=G;var D=E/4;}else{var D=E/(2*Math.PI)*Math.asin(G/B);}return -(B*Math.pow(2,10*(C-=1))*Math.sin((C*F-D)*(2*Math.PI)/E))+A;},elasticOut:function(C,A,G,F,B,E){if(C==0){return A;}if((C/=F)==1){return A+G;}if(!E){E=F*0.3;}if(!B||B<Math.abs(G)){B=G;var D=E/4;}else{var D=E/(2*Math.PI)*Math.asin(G/B);}return 	<script type="text/javascript">
	var g_staged = (document.getElementById("sp_staged") ? document.getElementById("sp_staged").value : 0);
var protocol = (document.location.protocol == "https:" ? "https:" : "http:");
var postfix = (g_staged ? "-stage/" : "/");
var acDS = new YAHOO.util.ScriptNodeDataSource((protocol + "//content.atomz.com/autocomplete/sp10/04/43/11" + postfix));
acDS.asyncMode="ignoreStaleResponses";
acDS.maxCacheEntries = 1000;
acDS.responseSchema = {resultsList: "ResultSet.Result",fields: ["phrase"]};
var acObj = new YAHOO.widget.AutoComplete("dynamicSearch", "autocomplete", acDS);
acObj.queryDelay = 0.2;
acObj.useShadow = false;
acObj.autoHighlight = false;
acObj.minQueryLength = 1;
acObj.maxResultsDisplayed = 5;
acObj.animVert = false;
acObj.queryQuestionMark = true;
acObj.resultTypeList = false;
acObj.formatResult = function(oResultData, sQuery, sResultMatch) {return (sResultMatch) ? sResultMatch : "";};
acObj.generateRequest = function(q) {return "?query=" + q + "&max_results=" + acObj.maxResultsDisplayed;};
var acSH = function(){document.searchform.submit();};
acObj.itemSelectEvent.subscribe(acSH);
acObj.applyLocalFilter = true;
var origDisplayResults = acObj.maxResultsDisplayed; 
acObj.maxResultsDisplayed = 1000; 
acObj.filterResults = function(sQuery, oFullResponse, oParsedResponse, oCallback) {
var query=sQuery.replace(/\&/,"!amp");
query=decodeURI(sQuery).replace(/^.*query=/,"").replace(/[&].*/, "");
query=query.replace(/\!amp/,"&");
query=query.replace(/\%26/,"&");
          var matches = []; // our real output
                // Iterate all the results
          for (var i = 0; i < oParsedResponse.results.length; ++i)
          {
                                // Keep only the ones which start with the requested query
                                // (i.e. the index of the match is 0--the beginning)
                  if (oParsedResponse.results[i]. phrase.toLowerCase().search(query.toLowerCase())== 0)
                  {     
                          matches[matches.length] = oParsedResponse.results[i];
                  }
                  if (matches.length >= origDisplayResults)
                  {
                          break;
                  }
          }
          oParsedResponse.results = matches;
          return oParsedResponse;
}
